  What I found

  - sentencinganalysis/ is a Flask app intended for Render. readme.md documents env vars, PACER/PCL auth, and the API endpoints. render.yaml
    shows multiple Render services (web/worker/cron/postgres/admin tools), pointing at https://github.com/carbidethegreate/sentencinganalysis.
  - Sample Pacer files and Pacer API Instructions/ is a reference bundle. PACER_FOLDER_SUMMARY.md summarizes PACER auth flow + PCL endpoints;
    includes PDFs, XSDs, and a TOTP sample app. This folder is the authoritative PACER/PCL spec reference for auth + API shape.
  - Repos that might be helpful to look at for reference /Pacer_1_migh_be_helpful/Untitled/ contains:
      - pacer1001/ – Python “pacer-docket-parser” project for parsing PACER docket PDFs into JSON/CSV.
      - pacer1003/ – R package pacerR for PACER XML retrieval; strong fee warnings and auth usage.
      - PacerSample1000/ – a bare git folder, no visible files besides .git.

  How this connects to the current Render log/export work

  - The running Render services from render.yaml match your stated service IDs (web + worker + cron + pserv). This is likely the same stack
    that the log-export script is hitting.
  - The PACER/PCL references clarify the expected authentication headers and environments used in your app (PACER_AUTH_BASE_URL, PCL_BASE_URL),
    which is relevant to the database/log errors you pasted.
  - The pacer-docket-parser and pacerR repos are for parsing or retrieving PACER data, not for Render log export. They’re useful once logs are
    downloaded or if you want to process docket PDFs/XL data.

• Here’s my recommendation based on the repo, our prior chat, and those sample repos:

  1. Primary path: keep using your current docket enrichment flow (HTML/XML), and extend it

  - You already fetch the docket report and parse entries in sentencinganalysis/docket_enrichment.py.
  - Extend _extract_docket_entries_from_html to capture:
      - filing date
      - ECF/document number
      - docket text/description
      - document link(s) (hrefs) so you can download later
  - Store those links in docket_entries JSON. That gives you a clean, searchable structure now and a path to future downloads.

  2. Use pacer1001 only for PDF docket parsing

  - pacer1001 is specifically built for PDF docket reports.
  - It’s useful if you later download docket PDFs and need to parse them into structured entries.
  - It doesn’t replace your current HTML/XML parsing; it’s a fallback if XML/HTML is unreliable.

  3. Use pacer1003 only if you want an external PACER XML pull

  - pacer1003 is an R package for PACER XML retrieval and network discovery.
  - It’s not an easy fit inside your Python/Flask pipeline.
  - It’s good as a research reference (auth flow, fee handling), not for production integration here.

  4. PacerSample1000 isn’t actionable

  - It only contains a .git directory; no usable code.

  If you want, I can proceed with the HTML docket entry extraction + link capture directly in your codebase. That’s the most practical next
  step to get structured, searchable docket text and enable later downloads.

• Thanks—clear. Here’s how I’d structure it given your end‑goal (PACER → full docket → AI analysis → attorney workflows):

  Core pipeline (recommended)

  1. PACER/PCL search (single + batch)
      - Use PCL API for batch case discovery and indexing.
      - Store case metadata, parties, court, judge, dates.
  2. Docket enrichment (HTML/XML)
      - For each case, fetch docket report (XML preferred, HTML fallback).
      - Parse header fields (judge, attorneys, parties, case type, assigned judges, filings).
      - Parse entries (date, ECF #, text, document links).
      - Store raw HTML, clean text, and structured entries.
  3. Document retrieval (optional on demand)
      - Store document links + metadata now.
      - Later: pull PDFs only when requested (avoids fees + storage bloat).
  4. AI analysis layer
      - Build an “extractor” job: summarize docket text and identify sentencing‑related signals (guidelines, criminal history, 5K1.1, plea
        terms, etc.).
      - Store model outputs as structured fields + citations to docket entries.
  5. Attorney UX
      - Connect PACER account per attorney (token + client code).
      - Case lookup + “attach case” to client.
      - Docket/filing timeline, AI reports, drafting tools, stored documents.

  ———

  What I’d implement first (based on current code)

  1. Extend HTML docket parsing to capture:
      - filing date
      - ECF/document number
      - docket text
      - document links (for future download)
  2. Extract header fields from the query/summary HTML you pasted (judge, last filing date, parties, attorneys, etc.).
  3. Store clean text + structured fields separately from raw HTML.

  That gives you a usable searchable docket and a clean base for AI.

  ———

  A few key schema suggestions

  - docket_entries JSON:
    {dateFiled, documentNumber, description, documentLinks:[{href, label}]}
  - docket_text_clean (plain text)
  - docket_html_raw (full HTML)
  - docket_header_fields (judge, case status, parties, attorneys, etc.)

  ———

  Clarifying questions before I code

  1. Do you want document links saved now (no downloads), or to add a download worker?
  2. Should we store AI outputs per case (summary + extracted facts) in pcl_case_fields, or create a new table (case_ai_insights)?
  3. Do you want header fields parsed into separate fields now (judge, attorneys, etc.), or just added to clean text?

     10 +
     11 +
     12 +@dataclass(frozen=True)
     13 +class DocumentJob:
     14 +    id: int
     15 +    case_id: int
     16 +    status: str
     17 +    documents_total: Optional[int]
     18 +    documents_downloaded: Optional[int]
     19 +
     20 +
     21 +class DocketDocumentWorker:
     22 +    def __init__(
     23 +        self,
     24 +        engine,
     25 +        tables: Dict[str, Table],
     26 +        *,
     27 +        http_client: Any,
     28 +        logger: Optional[Any] = None,
     29 +        documents_dir: Optional[str] = None,
     30 +    ) -> None:
     31 +        self._engine = engine
     32 +        self._tables = tables
     33 +        self._http_client = http_client
     34 +        self._logger = logger
     35 +        self._documents_dir = documents_dir or os.path.join(os.getcwd(), "pacer_documents")
     36 +
     37 +    def run_job(self, job_id: int, max_docs: int = 50) -> int:
     38 +        job = self._load_job(job_id)
     39 +        if not job:
     40 +            return 0
     41 +        if job["status"] not in {"queued", "running"}:
     42 +            return 0
     43 +        job = self._mark_running(job)
     44 +        processed = 0
     45 +        items = self._load_items(job["id"], max_docs=max_docs)
     46 +        for item in items:
     47 +            if item["status"] != "queued":
     48 +                continue
     49 +            try:
     50 +                self._download_item(job, item)
     51 +            except Exception as exc:
     52 +                self._mark_item_failed(item, str(exc))
     53 +            processed += 1
     54 +        self._finalize_job(job)
     55 +        return processed
     56 +
     57 +    def _load_job(self, job_id: int) -> Optional[Dict[str, Any]]:
     58 +        job_table = self._tables["docket_document_jobs"]
     59 +        with self._engine.begin() as conn:
     60 +            row = (
     61 +                conn.execute(select(job_table).where(job_table.c.id == job_id))
     62 +                .mappings()
     63 +                .first()
     64 +            )
     65 +        return dict(row) if row else None
     66 +
     67 +    def _load_items(self, job_id: int, max_docs: int) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
     68 +        items_table = self._tables["docket_document_items"]
     69 +        with self._engine.begin() as conn:
     70 +            rows = (
     71 +                conn.execute(
     72 +                    select(items_table)
     73 +                    .where(items_table.c.job_id == job_id)
     74 +                    .order_by(items_table.c.id.asc())
     75 +                    .limit(max_docs)
     76 +                )
     77 +                .mappings()
     78 +                .all()
     79 +            )
     80 +        return [dict(row) for row in rows]
     81 +
     82 +    def _mark_running(self, job: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
     83 +        job_table = self._tables["docket_document_jobs"]
     84 +        now = datetime.utcnow()
     85 +        updates = {"status": "running", "started_at": now, "last_error": None}
     86 +        with self._engine.begin() as conn:
     87 +            conn.execute(
     88 +                update(job_table).where(job_table.c.id == job["id"]).values(**updates)
     89 +            )
     90 +        job.update(updates)
     91 +        return job
     92 +
     93 +    def _mark_item_failed(self, item: Dict[str, Any], message: str) -> None:
     94 +        items_table = self._tables["docket_document_items"]
     95 +        now = datetime.utcnow()
     96 +        updates = {"status": "failed", "error": message, "updated_at": now}
     97 +        with self._engine.begin() as conn:
     98 +            conn.execute(
     99 +                update(items_table).where(items_table.c.id == item["id"]).values(**updates)
    100 +            )
    101 +        if self._logger:
    102 +            self._logger.warning("Document download failed: %s", message)
    103 +
    104 +    def _download_item(self, job: Dict[str, Any], item: Dict[str, Any]) -> None:
    105 +        url = item.get("source_url")
    106 +        if not url:
    107 +            raise ValueError("Missing source URL for document.")
    108 +        response = self._http_client.request(
    109 +            "GET",
    110 +            url,
    111 +            headers={"Accept": "application/pdf"},
    112 +            include_cookie=True,
    113 +        )
    114 +        if response.status_code != 200:
    115 +            raise ValueError(f"Download failed with status {response.status_code}.")
    116 +        content_type = response.headers.get("Content-Type", "")
    117 +        filename = _build_filename(
    118 +            job["case_id"],
    119 +            item.get("document_number"),
    120 +            item["id"],
    121 +            content_type=content_type,
    122 +        )
    123 +        target_dir = os.path.join(self._documents_dir, f"case_{job['case_id']}")
    124 +        os.makedirs(target_dir, exist_ok=True)
    125 +        target_path = os.path.join(target_dir, filename)
    126 +        with open(target_path, "wb") as handle:
    127 +            handle.write(response.body)
    128 +        items_table = self._tables["docket_document_items"]
    129 +        now = datetime.utcnow()
    130 +        updates = {
    131 +            "status": "downloaded",
    132 +            "file_path": target_path,
    133 +            "content_type": content_type,
    134 +            "bytes": len(response.body),
    135 +            "downloaded_at": now,
    136 +            "updated_at": now,
    137 +            "error": None,
    138 +        }
    139 +        with self._engine.begin() as conn:
    140 +            conn.execute(
    141 +                update(items_table)
    142 +                .where(items_table.c.id == item["id"])
    143 +                .values(**updates)
    144 +            )
    145 +
    146 +    def _finalize_job(self, job: Dict[str, Any]) -> None:
    147 +        items_table = self._tables["docket_document_items"]
    148 +        job_table = self._tables["docket_document_jobs"]
    149 +        with self._engine.begin() as conn:
    150 +            total = int(
    151 +                conn.execute(
    152 +                    select(items_table.c.id).where(items_table.c.job_id == job["id"])
    153 +                ).rowcount
    154 +                or 0
    155 +            )
    156 +            downloaded = conn.execute(
    157 +                select(items_table.c.id).where(
    158 +                    (items_table.c.job_id == job["id"])
    159 +                    & (items_table.c.status == "downloaded")
    160 +                )
    161 +            ).rowcount
    162 +            now = datetime.utcnow()
    163 +            status = "completed"
    164 +            updates = {
    165 +                "documents_total": total,
    166 +                "documents_downloaded": downloaded,
    167 +                "finished_at": now,
    168 +                "status": status,
    169 +                "updated_at": now,
    170 +            }
    171 +            conn.execute(
    172 +                update(job_table).where(job_table.c.id == job["id"]).values(**updates)
    173 +            )
    174 +
    175 +
    176 +def _build_filename(
    177 +    case_id: int,
    178 +    doc_number: Optional[str],
    179 +    item_id: int,
    180 +    *,
    181 +    content_type: str,
    182 +) -> str:
    183 +    ext = ".pdf"
    184 +    if "text/html" in (content_type or "").lower():
    185 +        ext = ".html"
    186 +    if doc_number:
    187 +        safe = re.sub(r"[^a-zA-Z0-9_-]+", "_", str(doc_number))
    188 +        return f"case_{case_id}_doc_{safe}_{item_id}{ext}"
    189 +    return f"case_{case_id}_doc_{item_id}{ext}"

    487 +def _load_document_jobs(conn, tables, detail: Dict[str, Any]) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
    488 +    jobs_table = tables.get("docket_document_jobs")
    489 +    items_table = tables.get("docket_document_items")
    490 +    case_id = detail.get("id")
    491 +    if jobs_table is None or not case_id:
    492 +        return []
    493 +    job_rows = (
    494 +        conn.execute(
    495 +            select(jobs_table)
    496 +            .where(jobs_table.c.case_id == case_id)
    497 +            .order_by(desc(jobs_table.c.created_at), desc(jobs_table.c.id))
    498 +            .limit(25)
    499 +        )
    500 +        .mappings()
    501 +        .all()
    502 +    )
    503 +    jobs = [dict(row) for row in job_rows]
    504 +    if not items_table or not jobs:
    505 +        return jobs
    506 +    job_ids = [job["id"] for job in jobs]
    507 +    item_rows = (
    508 +        conn.execute(
    509 +            select(items_table)
    510 +            .where(items_table.c.job_id.in_(job_ids))
    511 +            .order_by(items_table.c.id.asc())
    512 +        )
    513 +        .mappings()
    514 +        .all()
    515 +    )
    516 +    items_by_job: Dict[int, List[Dict[str, Any]]] = {}
    517 +    for row in item_rows:
    518 +        item = dict(row)
    519 +        items_by_job.setdefault(item["job_id"], []).append(item)
    520 +    for job in jobs:
    521 +        job["items"] = items_by_job.get(job["id"], [])

    2256 +        for field in case_fields or []:

• Pushed the “go” changes end‑to‑end: detailed PACER form logging + a full document download pipeline (queue + run + UI) with DB tables and
  admin controls.

  What I implemented

  - Form logging: when PACER returns a docket form, the last_error now includes form_action and key form fields (so we can debug the exact
    flow).
  - Document download pipeline:
      - New tables: docket_document_jobs, docket_document_items
      - New worker: DocketDocumentWorker to download documents using PACER session cookies
      - Admin endpoints: queue, download‑now, and run‑job
      - Case detail UI: queue/download buttons + job/item status tables
  - Migration added for the new tables.

  Files changed/added

  - sentencinganalysis/docket_enrichment.py
      - Adds form‑action/payload to errors for docket‑form responses.
  - sentencinganalysis/docket_documents.py (new)
      - Download worker + file storage logic.
  - sentencinganalysis/pcl_models.py
      - Added new tables.
  - sentencinganalysis/pcl_queries.py
      - Loads document jobs/items into case detail.
  - sentencinganalysis/app.py
      - Queue/download endpoints + helper functions.
  - sentencinganalysis/templates/admin_pcl_case_detail.html
      - Docket Documents UI.
  - sentencinganalysis/migrations/2026_01_27_docket_documents.sql (new)

  How to use (once migrated)

  - Case page → “Docket documents”
      - Queue document downloads (creates a job)
      - Download now (queues + immediately runs)
      - Run job (manually re‑run a queued/failed job)

  Notes

  - Downloads save under PACER_DOCUMENTS_DIR if set; otherwise ./pacer_documents/case_<id>/...
  - Jobs are marked completed_with_errors if any document fails; the job’s last_error is populated.

  Next steps (you can run)

  2. Re‑pull docket for a case and then use “Download now” to confirm docs are captured
  3. Share a new last_error if PACER still returns a form; it will now include actionable form details

  		var IsForm = false;
  		var FirstField;
  		function SetFocus() {
  			if(IsForm) {
  				if(FirstField) {
  					var ind = FirstField.indexOf('document.',0);
  					if(ind == 0)
  					{
  						eval(FirstField);
  					}
  					else
  					{
  						var Code = "document.forms[0]."+FirstField+".focus();";
  						eval(Code);
  					}
  				} else {
  					var Cnt = 0;
  					while(document.forms[0].elements[Cnt] != null) {
  						try {
  							if(document.forms[0].elements[Cnt].type != "hidden" &&
  									!document.forms[0].elements[Cnt].disabled &&
  									!document.forms[0].elements[Cnt].readOnly) {
  								document.forms[0].elements[Cnt].focus();
  								break;
  							}
  						}
  						catch(e) {}
  						Cnt += 1;
  					}
  				}
  			}
  			return(true);
  		}

• The current code misclassifies bankruptcy docket reports as shells because its report detection requires phrases absent in bankruptcy HTML.
  I'll update the report detection logic to recognize bankruptcy by checking for the "Docket Text" table with class "DktRpt" and adjust the
  shell detection to accommodate this so docket entries get properly extracted.

  Refining bankruptcy docket parsing

  I'm updating detection to identify bankruptcy reports by presence of "Docket Text," "Filing Date," and class "DktRpt," and adjusting row
  parsing to handle 4-cell tables where document number and description shift columns. Header rows with "Filing Date" and "Docket Text" will be
  correctly skipped, and links extraction will handle the amended cell structure. These changes ensure accurate docket entry extraction from
  bankruptcy reports.

    923 +    if "docket text" in lowered and "filing date" in lowered:
    924 +        return True
    925 +    if "docket text" in lowered and "u.s. bankruptcy court" in lowered:
    926 +        return True
    927 +    return False
    928

─ Worked for 57s ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

• You’re hitting a bankruptcy docket report format that our HTML parser was misclassifying as a “form,” so it never stored the docket text.
  I’ve updated the parser to correctly recognize and extract bankruptcy dockets like the sample you pasted.

  What I changed

  - Treats Bankruptcy docket reports as real reports (not forms)
  - Parses the bankruptcy table layout (Filing Date | # | Docket Text) correctly
  - Skips the header row properly and extracts:
      - Filing Date
      - ECF #
      - Docket Text
      - Document links

  File updated

  - sentencinganalysis/docket_enrichment.py

  Why it failed before

  - _looks_like_docket_report() only recognized “civil/criminal” formats.
  - Bankruptcy reports have “Filing Date / Docket Text” and a different table structure.
  - The parser was reading the wrong columns and marking the whole response as a “form.”

  Next step to see the fix

  1. Click Clear docket fields on the case page
  2. Re‑run docket enrichment for that case
  3. The docket entries should populate (date / ECF / text / links)

  If you want, send me the civil/criminal examples too—I can fine‑tune the parser for those edge cases as well.

• Got it — thanks for clarifying. Yes, the HTML you pasted is from the real PACER CM/ECF site, and it is a valid docket report (not a form).
  The parser now handles both:

  - Bankruptcy layout (Filing Date | # | Docket Text)
  - Criminal/Civil layout (Date Filed | # | Docket Text with “CRIMINAL DOCKET FOR CASE” header)

  So the parser should extract entries from that criminal sample once the system actually receives the report (not the form).

  Why you’re still seeing “Query / Reports / Docket Sheet…”

  - That page is the docket request form (not the report).
  - When we get that form, the job fails with “PACER returned a docket form instead of the docket report.”
  - That means PACER never delivered the report HTML yet (so there’s nothing to parse).

  What I need from you to solve it

  - Re‑run the docket pull after deploy, then send the new last_error string.
    It will now include form_action and form_keys, which tells me exactly how to submit the form for that court.

  About pcl-api-reports.xsd

  - Yes, I saw it.
  - It defines the PCL report metadata schema: reportId, status, time range, recordCount, pages, fees, criteria, and sort orders.
  - It’s for PCL batch report metadata, not CM/ECF docket HTML parsing — but it’s useful for validating PCL report receipts and batch status.

  Next steps (please do in this order)

  1. Deploy the latest code changes.
  2. Clear docket fields on the case page.
  3. Re‑pull the docket.
  4. Send me the new last_error text.

  If you want, I can also add a fallback that captures and stores the entire form HTML so we can reproduce the exact POST flow even faster.

  		var IsForm = false;
  		var FirstField;
  		function SetFocus() {
  			if(IsForm) {
  				if(FirstField) {
  					var ind = FirstField.indexOf('document.',0);
  					if(ind == 0)
  					{
  						eval(FirstField);
  					}
  					else
  					{
  						var Code = "document.forms[0]."+FirstField+".focus();";
  						eval(Code);
  					}
  				} else {
  					var Cnt = 0;
  					while(document.forms[0].elements[Cnt] != null) {
  						try {
  							if(document.forms[0].elements[Cnt].type != "hidden" &&
  									!document.forms[0].elements[Cnt].disabled &&
  									!document.forms[0].elements[Cnt].readOnly) {
  								document.forms[0].elements[Cnt].focus();
  								break;
  							}
  						}
  						catch(e) {}
  						Cnt += 1;
  					}
  				}
  			}
  			return(true);
  		}

      function ValidateAllOnSubmit(function_name,form_num) {
          if(form_num == null) form_num = 0; // default if not provided
          var f = document.forms[form_num];  // f is the form object

  	// anticipate programmer errors - if no quotes around 1st param, its a function reference
  	if(typeof(function_name) == "function")
  	    function_name = function_name.toString().match(/function\s+([^\(]+)/)[1];

  	// iterate through all the elements of the form
  	for(var i=0; i<f.length; i++)   {
  	    var e=f.elements[i];
  	    if (e.type=="text"  || e.type=="textarea") {
  		// adding foo on to onchange property of form element[i]
  		// because cant be null for pattern match
  		var msg=(e.onchange)+"foo";

  		// if the onchange attribute matches the function name (and optionally an arg list)
  		re = new RegExp(function_name+"(\\s*\\([^)]+\\))?"); // think of each \\ as \
  		var match = msg.match(re);
  		if  (match) {
                      function_call = match[0];

  		    // Execute validation function in question and see if it failed
                      function_call = function_call.replace(/this/g
                                             , "document.forms["+form_num+"].elements["+i+"]");
                      if(! eval(function_call)) {
  			e.focus();
  			return(false);
  		    }
  		}
  	    }
  	}
  	return(1);
      }
      </SCRIPT>

  		<script language="JavaScript">
  			var show_formats = function (action) {
  				var disable = false;
  				if (action == true) {
  					// Disable.
  					disable = true;
  					}
  				else if (action == false) {
  					// Enable.
  					disable = false;
  				}
  				else {
  					// Called by an event.
  					if (document.forms[0].schedule_id) {
  						disable = document.forms[0].schedule_id.value;
  					}
  					else {
  						disable = false;
  					}
  				}
  				var output_format=document.getElementById('output_format_radio_buttons');
  				if (output_format) {
  					document.forms[0].output_format[0].checked=true;
  					output_format.style.display=(disable ? 'none': 'inline');
  				}
  			}
  			CMECF.util.Event.addListener('schedule_id', 'change', show_formats);
  			CMECF.util.Event.addListener(window, 'load', show_formats);

  				}
  			}

  			var Rest_Seal_Entries = function (action) {
  			 if (action == true) {
  				if (document.getElementById("restricted_entries")) {
  					document.getElementById("restricted_entries").checked = true;
  				}
  				if (document.getElementById("sealed_entries")) {
  					document.getElementById("sealed_entries").checked = true;
  				}
  			 }
  			 if (action == false) {
  				if (document.getElementById("restricted_entries")) {
  					document.getElementById("restricted_entries").checked = false;
  				}
  				if (document.getElementById("sealed_entries")) {
  					document.getElementById("sealed_entries").checked = false;
  				}
  			 }
  			}

  			function PreResetProc() {
  				if (document.getElementById("vmd_vaa")) { document.getElementById("vmd_vaa").style.display = 'none'; }
  				if (document.getElementById("PreResetField").value === 'create_roa') {
  					document.getElementById('create_roa').checked = true;
  					document.getElementById('create_roa').disabled = false;
  					Disable_Tied_Checkbox('create_roa','create_appendix');
  					Disable_Tied_Checkbox('create_roa','create_abridged_docket_report');
  					Disable_Tied_Checkbox('create_roa','view_multi_docs');
  					show_roa(true);
  					show_appendix(false);
  					show_formats(true);
  					if (document.getElementById("court_user_roa")) {
  						Rest_Seal_Entries(false);
  					}
  				} else if(document.getElementById("PreResetField").value === 'create_appendix') {
  					document.getElementById('create_appendix').checked = true;
  					document.getElementById('create_appendix').disabled = false;
  					Disable_Tied_Checkbox('create_appendix','create_roa');
  					Disable_Tied_Checkbox('create_appendix','create_abridged_docket_report');
  					Disable_Tied_Checkbox('create_appendix','view_multi_docs');
  					if (document.getElementById('create_roa')) show_roa(false);
  					show_appendix(true);
  					show_formats(true);
  					if (document.getElementById("court_user")) {
  						Rest_Seal_Entries(false);
  					}
  				} else if(document.getElementById("PreResetField").value === 'view_multi_docs') {
  					document.getElementById('view_multi_docs').checked = true;
  					document.getElementById('view_multi_docs').disabled = false;
  					document.getElementById('pdf_header').disabled = false;
  					Disable_Tied_Checkbox('view_multi_docs','create_abridged_docket_report');
  					Disable_Tied_Checkbox('view_multi_docs','create_roa');
  					Disable_Tied_Checkbox('view_multi_docs','create_appendix');
  					show_formats(true);
  					if (document.getElementById('create_appendix')) show_appendix(false);
  					if (document.getElementById('create_roa'))  show_roa(false);
  					if (document.getElementById("vmd_vaa")) { document.getElementById("vmd_vaa").style.display = 'inline'; }
  				} else if(document.getElementById("PreResetField").value === 'create_abridged_docket_report') {
  					document.getElementById('create_abridged_docket_report').checked = true;
  					document.getElementById('create_abridged_docket_report').disabled = false;
  					document.getElementById('pdf_header').disabled = false;
  					Disable_Tied_Checkbox('create_abridged_docket_report', 'view_multi_docs');
  					Disable_Tied_Checkbox('create_abridged_docket_report', 'create_roa');
  					Disable_Tied_Checkbox('create_abridged_docket_report', 'create_appendix');
  					show_formats(true);
  					if (document.getElementById('create_appendix')) show_appendix(false);
  					if (document.getElementById('create_roa'))  show_roa(false);
  				} else {
  					if ((document.getElementById("PreResetFields").value).match('restricted_entries')) {
  						if (document.getElementById("restricted_entries")) {
  							document.getElementById("restricted_entries").checked = true;
  							document.getElementById("restricted_entries").disabled = false;
  						}
  					}
  					if ((document.getElementById("PreResetFields").value).match('sealed_entries')) {
  						if (document.getElementById("sealed_entries")) {
  							document.getElementById("sealed_entries").checked = true;
  							document.getElementById("sealed_entries").disabled = false;
  						}
  					}
  					if (document.getElementById('create_roa')) {
  						document.getElementById('create_roa').disabled = false;
  						show_roa(false);
  					}
  					if (document.getElementById('create_appendix')) {
  						document.getElementById('create_appendix').disabled = false;
  						show_appendix(false);
  					}
  					if (document.getElementById('pdf_header')) document.getElementById('pdf_header').disabled = false;
  					if (document.getElementById('view_multi_docs')) document.getElementById('view_multi_docs').disabled = false;
  					if (document.getElementById('create_abridged_docket_report')) document.getElementById('create_abridged_docket_report').disabled = false;
  					show_formats(false);
  				}
  			}

  			function PreResetlist() {

  <SCRIPT LANGUAGE="JavaScript">
  		var timerId;
  		var BeenHere = 0;
  		IsForm  = true;
  		function empty(s) {
  			var whitespace = " \t\n\r";
  			if(s == null || s.length == 0) {
  				return(true);
  			}
  		    // Is s only whitespace characters?
  		    for (var i = 0; i < s.length; i++) {
  		        var c = s.charAt(i);
         			 if (whitespace.indexOf(c) == -1) return false;
  		    }
  			return(true);
  		}
  		function ClearTimer() {
  			BeenHere = 0;
  			clearTimeout(timerId);
  			return(true);
  		}
  		var FormId = 0;
  		function ProcessForm() {
  			if(BeenHere == 1) {
  				alert("Submission already made, please wait for response from server");
  				return(false);
  			}
  			BeenHere = 1;
  			timerId=setTimeout("ClearTimer()",5000);
  if( ! ValidateAllOnSubmit("CheckDate", 0) ) {ClearTimer();return false;}
  if( ! ValidateAllOnSubmit("CheckNumber", 0) ) {ClearTimer();return false;}
  document.forms[FormId].submit();return true
  }

  function RunAfterClear() {
  	
  }

  <script language="JavaScript">
  var AssignResetButtonTimeout;
  function AssignResetButton() {
  	if (AssignResetButtonTimeout)
  		window.clearTimeout(AssignResetButtonTimeout);

  	var resetButton = document.forms[0].reset;
  	if (resetButton && resetButton.value) {
  		var oldHandler = resetButton.onclick;
  		var newHandler = function() {setTimeout("RunAfterClear()", 100)};
  		resetButton.onclick = function() {
  			if (oldHandler) {
  				oldHandler();
  			}
  			newHandler();
  		}
  	}
  	else
  		AssignResetButtonTimeout = window.setTimeout(AssignResetButton, 1);
  }
  AssignResetButton();
  </script>

  		var IsForm = false;
  		var FirstField;
  		function SetFocus() {
  			if(IsForm) {
  				if(FirstField) {
  					var ind = FirstField.indexOf('document.',0);
  					if(ind == 0)
  					{
  						eval(FirstField);
  					}
  					else
  					{
  						var Code = "document.forms[0]."+FirstField+".focus();";
  						eval(Code);
  					}
  				} else {
  					var Cnt = 0;
  					while(document.forms[0].elements[Cnt] != null) {
  						try {
  							if(document.forms[0].elements[Cnt].type != "hidden" &&
  									!document.forms[0].elements[Cnt].disabled &&
  									!document.forms[0].elements[Cnt].readOnly) {
  								document.forms[0].elements[Cnt].focus();
  								break;
  							}
  						}
  						catch(e) {}
  						Cnt += 1;
  					}
  				}
  			}
  			return(true);
  		}

      <SCRIPT>
      function ValidateAllOnSubmit(function_name,form_num) {
          if(form_num == null) form_num = 0; // default if not provided
          var f = document.forms[form_num];  // f is the form object

  	// anticipate programmer errors - if no quotes around 1st param, its a function reference
  	if(typeof(function_name) == "function")
  	    function_name = function_name.toString().match(/function\s+([^\(]+)/)[1];

  	// iterate through all the elements of the form
  	for(var i=0; i<f.length; i++)   {
  	    var e=f.elements[i];
  	    if (e.type=="text"  || e.type=="textarea") {
  		// adding foo on to onchange property of form element[i]
  		// because cant be null for pattern match
  		var msg=(e.onchange)+"foo";

  		// if the onchange attribute matches the function name (and optionally an arg list)
  		re = new RegExp(function_name+"(\\s*\\([^)]+\\))?"); // think of each \\ as \
  		var match = msg.match(re);
  		if  (match) {
                      function_call = match[0];

  		    // Execute validation function in question and see if it failed
                      function_call = function_call.replace(/this/g
                                             , "document.forms["+form_num+"].elements["+i+"]");
                      if(! eval(function_call)) {
  			e.focus();
  			return(false);
  		    }
  		}
  	    }
  	}
  	return(1);
      }
      </SCRIPT>

  		var timerId;

  		function empty(s) {
  			var whitespace = " \t\n\r";
  			if(s == null || s.length == 0) {
  				return(true);
  			}
  		    // Is s only whitespace characters?
  		    for (var i = 0; i < s.length; i++) {
  		        var c = s.charAt(i);
         			 if (whitespace.indexOf(c) == -1) return false;
  		    }
  			return(true);
  		}
  		function ClearTimer() {
  			BeenHere = 0;
  			clearTimeout(timerId);
  			return(true);
  		}
  		var FormId = 0;
  		function ProcessForm() {
  			if(BeenHere == 1) {
  				alert("Submission already made, please wait for response from server");
  				return(false);
  			}
  			BeenHere = 1;
  			timerId=setTimeout("ClearTimer()",5000);
  if( ! ValidateAllOnSubmit("CheckDate", 0) ) {ClearTimer();return false;}
  if( ! ValidateAllOnSubmit("CheckNumber", 0) ) {ClearTimer();return false;}
  document.forms[FormId].submit();return true
  }

  <script language="JavaScript">
  var AssignResetButtonTimeout;
  function AssignResetButton() {
  	if (AssignResetButtonTimeout)
  		window.clearTimeout(AssignResetButtonTimeout);

  	var resetButton = document.forms[0].reset;
  	if (resetButton && resetButton.value) {
  		var oldHandler = resetButton.onclick;

  			if (oldHandler) {

  			}

  		}
  	}

─ Worked for 1m 22s ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

• I’ve added a more robust fallback submit for this PACER form.

  Why it still failed

  - The form has no name on the case number input, so the server only gets data if we inject it.
  - Some courts accept formatted case numbers (3:25-mj-00099), others accept raw (3:2025mj00099), or even just the numeric ID.
  - Some courts also behave differently depending on whether all_case_ids is present or empty.

  What I changed (now)

  - The submit will try multiple variants automatically:
      - case_number_text_area_0 = formatted case number → raw full → raw short
      - all_case_ids = case_id → empty string → omitted
  - It stops as soon as it gets a response that is not the form.

  File updated

  - sentencinganalysis/docket_enrichment.py

  Next steps

  1. Deploy
  2. Clear docket fields
  3. Re‑run docket enrichment

  If it still returns the form after this, I’ll add a direct form override that bypasses the form entirely by POSTing the known case number and
  forcing output format. That’s the last fallback and should work even for these odd CM/ECF setups.

  Tell me the new result after you re‑run.

      function ValidateAllOnSubmit(function_name,form_num) {
          if(form_num == null) form_num = 0; // default if not provided
          var f = document.forms[form_num];  // f is the form object

  	// anticipate programmer errors - if no quotes around 1st param, its a function reference
  	if(typeof(function_name) == &#34;function&#34;)
  	    function_name = function_name.toString().match(/function\s+([^\(]+)/)[1];

  	// iterate through all the elements of the form
  	for(var i=0; i&lt;f.length; i++)   {
  	    var e=f.elements[i];
  	    if (e.type==&#34;text&#34;  || e.type==&#34;textarea&#34;) {
  		// adding foo on to onchange property of form element[i]
  		// because cant be null for pattern match
  		var msg=(e.onchange)+&#34;foo&#34;;

  		// if the onchange attribute matches the function name (and optionally an arg list)
  		re = new RegExp(function_name+&#34;(\\s*\\([^)]+\\))?&#34;); // think of each \\ as \
  		var match = msg.match(re);
  		if  (match) {
                      function_call = match[0];

  		    // Execute validation function in question and see if it failed
                      function_call = function_call.replace(/this/g
                                             , &#34;document.forms[&#34;+form_num+&#34;].elements[&#34;+i+&#34;]&#34;);
                      if(! eval(function_call)) {
  			e.focus();
  			return(false);
  		    }
  		}
  	    }
  	}
  	return(1);
      }

  &lt;SCRIPT LANGUAGE=&#34;JavaScript&#34;&gt;
  		var timerId;
  		var BeenHere = 0;
  		IsForm  = true;
  		function empty(s) {
  			var whitespace = &#34; \t\n\r&#34;;
  			if(s == null || s.length == 0) {
  				return(true);
  			}
  		    // Is s only whitespace characters?
  		    for (var i = 0; i &lt; s.length; i++) {
  		        var c = s.charAt(i);
         			 if (whitespace.indexOf(c) == -1) return false;
  		    }
  			return(true);
  		}
  		function ClearTimer() {
  			BeenHere = 0;
  			clearTimeout(timerId);
  			return(true);
  		}
  		var FormId = 0;
  		function ProcessForm() {
  			if(BeenHere == 1) {
  				alert(&#34;Submission already made, please wait for response from server&#34;);
  				return(false);
  			}
  			BeenHere = 1;
  			timerId=setTimeout(&#34;ClearTimer()&#34;,5000);
  if( ! ValidateAllOnSubmit(&#34;CheckDate&#34;, 0) ) {ClearTimer();return false;}
  if( ! ValidateAllOnSubmit(&#34;CheckNumber&#34;, 0) ) {ClearTimer();return false;}
  document.forms[FormId].submit();return true
  }

  function RunAfterClear() {
  	
  }
  &lt;/SCRIPT&gt;

  &lt;script language=&#34;JavaScript&#34;&gt;
  var AssignResetButtonTimeout;
  function AssignResetButton() {
  	if (AssignResetButtonTimeout)
  		window.clearTimeout(AssignResetButtonTimeout);

  	var resetButton = document.forms[0].reset;
  	if (resetButton &amp;&amp; resetButton.value) {
  		var oldHandler = resetButton.onclick;
  		var newHandler = function() {setTimeout(&#34;RunAfterClear()&#34;, 100)};
  		resetButton.onclick = function() {
  			if (oldHandler) {
  				oldHandler();
  			}
  			newHandler();
  		}
  	}
  	else
  		AssignResetButtonTimeout = window.setTimeout(AssignResetButton, 1);
  }
  AssignResetButton();
  &lt;/script&gt;

─ Worked for 42s ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

• Short answer: no, pcl-api-reports.xsd does not define a docket report endpoint you can call to get full docket text. It only defines report
  metadata and batch report wrappers for the PACER Case Locator (PCL) search APIs (cases/parties). There’s no “docket” element or docket‑entry
  payload in that XSD, and a full‑text docket isn’t part of the PCL schema set at all.

  What I found in your local docs:

  - pcl-api-reports.xsd → only report metadata (reportInfo, reportList, download) and sort info; no docket content.
  - pcl-api-cases.xsd + pcl-api-parties.xsd → case/party search results only.
  - PCL-API-Document_4.1.pdf → describes PCL search endpoints (cases/parties), not CM/ECF docket reports.
  - pacer_xml_apv3.1.pdf → CM/ECF Appellate XML only (appellate, not district/bk). It describes docket XML for appellate courts, but it’s not
    the PCL API and doesn’t cover district/bankruptcy CM/ECF dockets.
  - PACER_FOLDER_SUMMARY.md confirms the same: PCL is search, appellate XML is separate.

  So: there isn’t an official “PCL API” endpoint that returns the full docket text you’re after for district/bankruptcy/criminal cases. That’s
  why we’re walking the CM/ECF form flow (CaseSearch → CaseSummary → FullDocket → confirm charge → report).

  If you want, I can open the PDF (PCL-API-Document_4.1.pdf) and quote the exact sections that show there’s no docket report endpoint — but the
  XSD already confirms it.

  Do you want me to:

  1. Add a debug capture so we can see the exact PACER form POST/response headers for your failing case?
  2. Continue refining the CM/ECF flow to match the R reference flow (CaseSearch → CaseSummary → fullDocket → filter → confirm) for district
     courts?

› Introduction

  There are a lot of curiosities that you encounter while working with PACER. This document serves a spot to write them all down.

  Form Submissions

  So far, every form on PACER has been set to submit files, even though there are no files to be submitted. This means that in the HTML, you
  see things like:

  <FORM NAME=GetPass ENCTYPE='multipart/form-data' method=POST
            action="/cgi-bin/WrtOpRpt.pl">
  To submit such a form using Python requests is pretty messy, but the general idea is that it looks like:

  r = s.post(
      url,
      headers={'User-Agent': 'Juriscraper'},
      verify=certifi.where(),
      timeout=30,
      files={
          'login': ('', username),
          'key': ('', password)
      },
  )
  The weirdest part is that we're submitting form data (the keys, username and password) as if they are files. The empty strings in the files
  parameter are the filenames that would normally be submitted with these values. So in effect, the above submits two "files" with the keys
  login and key, and the contents of the "files" are your username and password.

  Yes, this is weird.

  Cookies

  The main cookie for PACER seems to be:

  PacerSession
  Which tends to have a value like:

  r77EsXg47bLdBZEdpPOmWMAA75FOBhJs4nr1bhcdCManBHTjfaFVPkqXkhENscRtylDzyXW2xnsVZrh6ZNljiaqQaZ0P86yzusAjT7naq9OhyQwDWvLCP0a5BAZ87T1C
  We've also seen evidence of these other cookies in the HTML of the Written Reports page for CAND:

  ClientDesc
  PacerClient
  PacerClientCode
  PacerPref
  PacerSession
  PublicTerminal
  REDIRECTINSIDE
  KEY
  doc1 URLs

  Every document in PACER can be accessed with what we call a doc-one URL. It looks like:

  https://ecf.nysd.uscourts.gov/doc1/12716951218
  This weird little URL has the following parts of interest:

  nysd: the jurisdiction of the item. These *mostly* correspond to the same
        IDs we have in CourtListener, but they occassionally differ.

  127:  The first three digits of the number at the end correspond to the
        court, with the earlier numbers going to circuit courts, and then the
        numbers being assigned alphabetically after that. For example, 127,
        above, corresponds to nysd. 128 corresponds to nywb.

  1:    The fourth digit in the URL indicates whether the item has attachments
        or not. If it does not have attachments, this number will be a 1, and
        you can download the item using the URL. If it does have attachments,
        the number will be a zero, and clicking it will take you to the
        attachments list. For items that have a zero, you can switch it to a 1
        to bypass the attachments list screen and simply get the item you're
        after.

        We always coerce this value to zero to avoid duplicates in our
        database.

  6951218: The remaining numbers appear to just be a serial number for each
        item. So far no patterns detected.
  It's my belief (mlr) that the doc1 URLs have this name because of their fourth digit.

  APIs

  possible_case_numbers.pl

  PACER has an API that you can use to look up case numbers and get case names and PACER docket IDs in XML as the result. This API is used by
  the main PACER query page when you past in a case number and press the button for "Find this Case". This needs further inspection, requests
  look like:

  GET 'https://ecf.cand.uscourts.gov/cgi-bin/possible_case_numbers.pl?3:12-cv-3879;number=0.1258953044538912'
  Which returns:

  <request number='3:12-cv-3879'>
      <case number='3:12-cv-3879'
            id='257622'
            title='3:12-cv-03879-VC Technology Properties Limited LLC et al v. Novatel Wireless, Inc. (closed 07/14/2015)'
            sortable='3:2012-cv-03879-VC'/>
  </request>
  The number=0.1258953044538912 parameter is used to defeat browser caching (cf. https://ecf.cand.uscourts.gov/lib/validate_case_number.js
  l.1499: "This random number causes the browser to never cache case number results."), so you can ignore it. Removing or tweaking it doesn't
  seem to make a difference.

  mobile_query.pl

  The mobile query page, e.g. https://ecf.mad.uscourts.gov/cgi-bin/mobile_query.pl, returns the number of docket entries in a case without
  charging a fee, as:

  <a id="entriesLink" href="/cgi-bin/mobile_query.pl?search=dktEntry&amp;caseid=191474&amp;caseNum=1:17-cv-11577-PBS" data-transition="slide"
  class="ui-link-inherit">
                              Docket Entries
                              <span class="ui-li-count ui-btn-up-c ui-btn-corner-all">
                                  52
                              </span>
                          </a>
  However, this count includes unnumbered minute entries. So the number may well be higher than the highest numbered docket entry in a case.

  DocVerify.pl

  This page is only available on CM/ECF, but provides several pieces of interesting information. This page is supposed to do some sort of
  document verification. As described in this handy PDF, you can input a case number and a document number from that case, and it will give
  you some hashes about that document. This sounds very useful as a form of verification, but it's entirely unclear what the hashes represent.

  The only use that the page seems to have is that it allows you to see if the current hashes (as computed by PACER) match the original hashes
  (as computed by PACER). I guess this helps you to understand whether the item has changed, but a simple "has this item changed" button seems
  more obvious.

  Anyway, the page also provides the docket entry text and file size, which is potentially quite useful.

  document_link.pl

  Now (apparently) deprecated from District CMECF, but possibly still current in Bankruptcy CMECF, an href link to a document in a Docket
  Report or Claims Register may come with an id property that encodes various link parameters, with K delimiting parameters (& function) and V
  delimiting assignments (= function). The CMECF.widget.DocLink() function (in dls_url.js, see below) calls document_link.pl to rewrite these
  into /doc1 URLs which are then bare of such metadata.

  For instance:

    <a
      href="/cgi-bin/show_doc.pl?caseid=605035&amp;claim_id=43976411&amp;claim_num=70-1&amp;magic_num=MAGIC"
      id="documentKcaseidV605035Kclaim_idV43976411Kclaim_numV70-1Kmagic_numVMAGIC">
      70-1
    </a>
    <script>
      CMECF.widget.DocLink('documentKcaseidV605035Kclaim_idV43976411Kclaim_numV70-1Kmagic_numVMAGIC');
    </script>
  whereupon

    https://ecf.caeb.uscourts.gov/cgi-bin/document_link.pl?documentKcaseidV605035Kclaim_idV43976411Kclaim_numV70-1Kmagic_numVMAGIC
  returns

    https://ecf.caeb.uscourts.gov/doc1/032026913922
  show_case_doc

  Discovered in the EDNY RSS feed, the show_case_doc script (no terminal .pl) allows looking up a doc1 URL (DLS) in District CMECF (no BK
  support) given the case ID and document number. E.g.:

    https://ecf.nyed.uscourts.gov/cgi-bin/show_case_doc?90,406590,,,
  returns a 302 redirect to

     https://ecf.nyed.uscourts.gov/doc1/123013711961?caseid=406590&pdf_header=2
  JavaScript on PACER

  All of the JavaScript in PACER has been compressed making it difficult to understand. However, you can often find a comment before the
  compressed file saying where the uncompressed version lives. In case that changes, here's the District goDLS function, as available here:
  https://ecf.mad.uscourts.gov/lib/dls_url.js:

  ////////////////////////////////////////
  // My understanding of the parameters //
  ////////////////////////////////////////
  // Generates a form, appends it to the end of the document, and then
  // submits it.
  //
  // hyperlink: Where the form is posted to. The HTML 'action' attribute.
  // de_caseid: The internal PACER ID for the case.
  // de_seqno: The internal PACER document number within the case. This
  //   differs from the number that we see for reasons unknown.
  // got_receipt: If set to '1', this will bypass the receipt page and
  //   download the PDF immediately. This is set to 1 *after* the user has
  //   seen the receipt. If receipts are disabled, I believe this will always
  //   be the empty string.
  // pdf_header: Whether to put the blue header on the top of the generated
  //  PDFs. 1 means to do so, 2 means to not do so. Some courts seem to
  //  treat the absence of this parameter as a desire not to do the header.
  // pdf_toggle_possible: ??
  // magic_num: ??
  // hdr: ??

  function goDLS(hyperlink, de_caseid, de_seqno, got_receipt, pdf_header, pdf_toggle_possible, magic_num, hdr) {
      var form_id  = 'go_dls_url';
      var form_element;

      if (document.getElementById(form_id)) {
          var old_form = document.getElementById(form_id);
          document.body.removeChild(old_form);
      }

      var url_form = document.createElement('form');
      url_form.setAttribute('action', hyperlink);
      url_form.setAttribute('enctype', 'multipart/form-data');
      url_form.setAttribute('method', 'post');
      url_form.setAttribute('id'	, form_id);
      document.body.appendChild(url_form);

      // optional additional parameters

      if (de_caseid.length > 0) {
          // always supplied when following links from application
          form_element = document.createElement('input');
          form_element.setAttribute('type', 'hidden');
          form_element.setAttribute('name', 'caseid');
          form_element.setAttribute('value', de_caseid);
          url_form.appendChild(form_element);
      }

      if (de_seqno.length > 0) {
          // always supplied when following links from application
          form_element = document.createElement('input');
          form_element.setAttribute('type', 'hidden');
          form_element.setAttribute('name', 'de_seq_num');
          form_element.setAttribute('value', de_seqno);
          url_form.appendChild(form_element);
      }

      if (got_receipt.length > 0) {
          // supplied from receipt page displayed before document viewing
          form_element = document.createElement('input');
          form_element.setAttribute('type', 'hidden');
          form_element.setAttribute('name', 'got_receipt');
          form_element.setAttribute('value', got_receipt);
          url_form.appendChild(form_element);
      }

      if (pdf_header.length > 0) {
          // optional user preference (overrideable by application defaults)
          form_element = document.createElement('input');
          form_element.setAttribute('type', 'hidden');
          form_element.setAttribute('name', 'pdf_header');
          form_element.setAttribute('value', pdf_header);
          url_form.appendChild(form_element);
      }

      if (pdf_toggle_possible.length > 0) {
          // optional user preference (overrideable by application defaults)
          form_element = document.createElement('input');
          form_element.setAttribute('type', 'hidden');
          form_element.setAttribute('name', 'pdf_toggle_possible');
          form_element.setAttribute('value', pdf_toggle_possible);
          url_form.appendChild(form_element);
      }

      if (magic_num.length > 0) {
          // only provided from application when NEF hyperlink clicked on multi-document filing
          form_element = document.createElement('input');
          form_element.setAttribute('type', 'hidden');
          form_element.setAttribute('name', 'magic_num');
          form_element.setAttribute('value', magic_num);
          url_form.appendChild(form_element);
      }

      if (hdr.length > 0) {
          // only provided from application when NEF hyperlink clicked on ROA/Appendix
          form_element = document.createElement('input');
          form_element.setAttribute('type', 'hidden');
          form_element.setAttribute('name', 'hdr');
          form_element.setAttribute('value', hdr);
          url_form.appendChild(form_element);
      }

      document.getElementById(form_id).submit();
  }
  In Bankruptcy CMECF, the function signature is different, replacing the hdr parameter with various bankruptcy-specific parameters for claim
  documents. https://ecf.caeb.uscourts.gov/lib/dls_url.js:

  function goDLS(hyperlink, de_caseid, de_seqno, got_receipt, pdf_header, pdf_toggle_possible, magic_num, claim_id, claim_num, claim_doc_seq)
  { here is another gitrepo that might be helpful

  handle these forms properly while preserving existing cookie handling.

  I'll also ask the user for the repo path to review the code directly.

• Yes — this is very helpful. It explains a few PACER behaviors that we’re not fully handling yet:

  Key takeaways I’d use immediately

  - multipart/form-data for form posts: the docket form is ENCTYPE='multipart/form-data'. We currently post application/x-www-form-urlencoded.
    Some CM/ECF installs are picky; we should switch to multipart when the form says so.
  - Extra cookies (PacerSession, KEY, PublicTerminal, etc.): we now persist Set-Cookie, but this confirms those cookies matter and should be
    preserved/sent on every request.
  - Doc links + goDLS: some links require the goDLS(...) POST payload or document_link.pl rewrite; we should parse/store those params for
    document downloads.
  - possible_case_numbers.pl: can be used to resolve case_id/title if needed.
  - show_case_doc: useful fallback to turn (case_id, doc #) into a doc1 URL.

  If you want me to implement this next, I’ll do:

  1. Multipart form submission for docket forms (no new deps; small encoder).
  2. Capture form enctype and choose multipart vs urlencoded.
  3. Parse goDLS params from onClick and store them with docket entries.
  4. Optional: add possible_case_numbers.pl lookup when case_id is missing or docket keeps returning form.

› NextGen CM/ECF XML Case Opening and Docketing
  The XML Case Opening module allows more data to be captured through an uploaded XML file and streamlines the data entry process for
  attorneys.

  This information is intended for bankruptcy petition preparation software vendors to open a bankruptcy case in NextGen CM/ECF, following the
  guidelines for XML submission of the bankruptcy petition and relevant documents, as defined in the Information Exchange Package
  Documentation (IEPD). Vendor software should be updated to communicate with NextGen CM/ECF web services and submit XML data, but also
  continue providing the PDF, which is the official record in the case. When a case has been opened with XML, the post-petition filing of
  missing or amended schedules, statements and/or other relevant forms should be filed with XML.

  IEPD for NextGen Bankruptcy Release 1.7 (zip) (11/16/2021)
  IEPD for NextGen Bankruptcy Release 1.6.x Hotfixes (zip) (11/16/2021)    - Developer Resources
  These resources provide technical documentation, downloads, and other information needed to extend the functionality of CM/ECF or developing
  other tools that interface with CM/ECF.

  Please note, this is not a complete compilation of the CM/ECF application created by the federal Judiciary. Many individual courts have
  modified the system to fit its needs. As a result, programming based on this information may not work in the same manner in every court's
  CM/ECF system. For information on modifications made by a specific court, please contact that court directly.

  Read the full CM/ECF developer disclaimer
  Sign up to receive developer resources updates by email.



  Technical Information
  Commercial PACER users who run data scraping scripts should do large data pulls between 6 p.m. and 6 a.m. Central Time. This helps reported
  intermittently slow system performance for other users. The federal Judiciary may suspend or reduce PACER access to any account causing an
  unacceptable level of operational disruption.

  Access CM/ECF Release Notes
  Access Release Notes for PACER-enabling Applications
  Individual court information, including links to CM/ECF, from the CM/ECF Court Lookup can be pulled using the following scripts:

  JSON feed
  XML feed
  Application Programming Interface (API)
  An API is a set of procedures that allows users to create applications that access the data and features of other applications, services, or
  operating systems. The following sections provide documentation and resources for using the PACER Authentication and PACER Case Locator
  (PCL) APIs.

  PACER Authentication API
  To access court records, the first step is to get an authentication token using your PACER username and password. The PACER Authentication
  API allows the user to authenticate automatically and without a user interface. This can help facilitate access for automated systems.

  The PACER Authentication API user manual provides documentation and examples on this process.

  PACER Case Locator (PCL) API
  The PACER Case Locator (PCL) is a nationwide index of federal court cases. The public PCL API allows users to programmatically search the
  PCL for federal cases or associated parties. This API uses the same search functionality as the PCL application and searches the same data
  set.

  The PCL API user manual provides documentation and examples on this process.

  Bankruptcy
  Review information and documentation for different features and functionality for the NextGen CM/ECF system.

  E-Filing of Bankruptcy Claims by Creditors
  Read the specifications describing processes for electronic filing of claims information in U.S. bankruptcy courts in a batch mode by
  creditors.

  CM/ECF Case Upload
  Case Upload allows attorneys to upload a text file created by commercial bankruptcy petition software to CM/ECF to complete the bankruptcy
  case opening process without filling out the CM/ECF case opening screens. Use the following technical information for instructions on using
  the feature:

  Bankruptcy Case Information File for Release 5.3.5/NextGen 1.5.4, 1.6.3, 1.7.0 and 1.7.1 (pdf) (7/11/2023)
  Case Upload also accepts the petition and may require a creditor matrix. If the case information is complete and the files are in the
  correct format, the module will complete the case opening process and display the notices of electronic filing. If the case information is
  incomplete or the files are not in the correct format, the system will display an error message, and the filer will be required to correct
  the problem before the case can be successfully opened.

  After opening the case, CM/ECF will docket the lead event and, if applicable, the chapter 13 plan and the certificate of credit counseling.
  If a creditor matrix was provided, Case Upload will also add the creditors to the new case. The notices of electronic filing show the case
  number that was automatically generated for the new case. In addition to the PDF documents uploaded on the initial screen, the court may
  automatically generate a 341 notice.

  varies by court. I'll note that for docket access, the CM/ECF UI flow with multipart/form-data and cookies is required, offer to implement
  these, and ask for the repo path if integration is desired.

  Summarizing PACER doc insights and proposing implementation

  I'll clarify that the resources focus on filing and case opening rather than docket retrieval, which requires scraping the CM/ECF UI using
  multipart/form-data and cookie handling. I'll propose implementing multipart posting and goDLS/document link parsing next and ask if the user
  wants to proceed, also requesting the repo path for integration context.

• Got it — thanks for sharing that. That text is developer resources, but it’s about filing/opening cases (XML Case Opening, Case Upload,
  creditor claims), plus PCL search and appellate‑only XML tags. It does not provide a documented API for district/bankruptcy docket retrieval.
  So it doesn’t replace the CM/ECF UI flow we’re using.

  What’s relevant from that excerpt to our problem:

  - Forms are multipart/form‑data even when they look like regular form posts.
    We currently post application/x-www-form-urlencoded. Some courts reject that and keep returning the form. We should switch to multipart
    when the form says ENCTYPE='multipart/form-data'.
  - Extra cookies matter (PacerSession, KEY, PublicTerminal, etc.).
    We now persist Set‑Cookie, but this confirms those cookies are required.
  - goDLS/document_link.pl logic is needed to get correct doc1 links and handle attachments.

  So the plan from this is:

  1. Submit PACER forms as multipart/form‑data when form enctype says so.

  		var IsForm = false;
  		var FirstField;
  		function SetFocus() {
  			if(IsForm) {
  				if(FirstField) {
  					var ind = FirstField.indexOf('document.',0);
  					if(ind == 0)
  					{
  						eval(FirstField);
  					}
  					else
  					{
  						var Code = "document.forms[0]."+FirstField+".focus();";
  						eval(Code);
  					}
  				} else {
  					var Cnt = 0;
  					while(document.forms[0].elements[Cnt] != null) {
  						try {
  							if(document.forms[0].elements[Cnt].type != "hidden" &&
  									!document.forms[0].elements[Cnt].disabled &&
  									!document.forms[0].elements[Cnt].readOnly) {
  								document.forms[0].elements[Cnt].focus();
  								break;
  							}
  						}
  						catch(e) {}
  						Cnt += 1;
  					}
  				}
  			}
  			return(true);
  		}

      <SCRIPT>
      function ValidateAllOnSubmit(function_name,form_num) {
          if(form_num == null) form_num = 0; // default if not provided
          var f = document.forms[form_num];  // f is the form object

  	// anticipate programmer errors - if no quotes around 1st param, its a function reference
  	if(typeof(function_name) == "function")
  	    function_name = function_name.toString().match(/function\s+([^\(]+)/)[1];

  	// iterate through all the elements of the form
  	for(var i=0; i<f.length; i++)   {
  	    var e=f.elements[i];
  	    if (e.type=="text"  || e.type=="textarea") {
  		// adding foo on to onchange property of form element[i]
  		// because cant be null for pattern match
  		var msg=(e.onchange)+"foo";

  		// if the onchange attribute matches the function name (and optionally an arg list)
  		re = new RegExp(function_name+"(\\s*\\([^)]+\\))?"); // think of each \\ as \
  		var match = msg.match(re);
  		if  (match) {
                      function_call = match[0];

  		    // Execute validation function in question and see if it failed
                      function_call = function_call.replace(/this/g
                                             , "document.forms["+form_num+"].elements["+i+"]");
                      if(! eval(function_call)) {
  			e.focus();
  			return(false);
  		    }
  		}
  	    }
  	}
  	return(1);
      }
      </SCRIPT>

  		function empty(s) {
  			var whitespace = " \t\n\r";
  			if(s == null || s.length == 0) {
  				return(true);
  			}
  		    // Is s only whitespace characters?
  		    for (var i = 0; i < s.length; i++) {
  		        var c = s.charAt(i);
         			 if (whitespace.indexOf(c) == -1) return false;
  		    }
  			return(true);
  		}

  			BeenHere = 0;
  			clearTimeout(timerId);
  			return(true);
  		}

  var AssignResetButtonTimeout;
  function AssignResetButton() {
  	if (AssignResetButtonTimeout)
  		window.clearTimeout(AssignResetButtonTimeout);

  	var resetButton = document.forms[0].reset;
  	if (resetButton && resetButton.value) {
  		var oldHandler = resetButton.onclick;
  		var newHandler = function() {setTimeout("RunAfterClear()", 100)};
  		resetButton.onclick = function() {
  			if (oldHandler) {
  				oldHandler();
  			}
  			newHandler();
  		}
  	}
  	else
  		AssignResetButtonTimeout = window.setTimeout(AssignResetButton, 1);
  }
  AssignResetButton();

  		var IsForm = false;
  		var FirstField;
  		function SetFocus() {
  			if(IsForm) {
  				if(FirstField) {
  					var ind = FirstField.indexOf('document.',0);
  					if(ind == 0)
  					{
  						eval(FirstField);
  					}
  					else
  					{
  						var Code = "document.forms[0]."+FirstField+".focus();";
  						eval(Code);
  					}
  				} else {
  					var Cnt = 0;
  					while(document.forms[0].elements[Cnt] != null) {
  						try {
  							if(document.forms[0].elements[Cnt].type != "hidden" &&
  									!document.forms[0].elements[Cnt].disabled &&
  									!document.forms[0].elements[Cnt].readOnly) {
  								document.forms[0].elements[Cnt].focus();
  								break;
  							}
  						}
  						catch(e) {}
  						Cnt += 1;
  					}
  				}
  			}
  			return(true);
  		}

      <SCRIPT>
      function ValidateAllOnSubmit(function_name,form_num) {
          if(form_num == null) form_num = 0; // default if not provided
          var f = document.forms[form_num];  // f is the form object

  	// anticipate programmer errors - if no quotes around 1st param, its a function reference
  	if(typeof(function_name) == "function")
  	    function_name = function_name.toString().match(/function\s+([^\(]+)/)[1];

  	// iterate through all the elements of the form
  	for(var i=0; i<f.length; i++)   {
  	    var e=f.elements[i];
  	    if (e.type=="text"  || e.type=="textarea") {
  		// adding foo on to onchange property of form element[i]
  		// because cant be null for pattern match
  		var msg=(e.onchange)+"foo";

  		// if the onchange attribute matches the function name (and optionally an arg list)
  		re = new RegExp(function_name+"(\\s*\\([^)]+\\))?"); // think of each \\ as \
  		var match = msg.match(re);
  		if  (match) {
                      function_call = match[0];

  		    // Execute validation function in question and see if it failed
                      function_call = function_call.replace(/this/g
                                             , "document.forms["+form_num+"].elements["+i+"]");
                      if(! eval(function_call)) {
  			e.focus();
  			return(false);
  		    }
  		}
  	    }
  	}
  	return(1);
      }
      </SCRIPT>

  			var show_formats = function (action) {
  				var disable = false;
  				if (action == true) {
  					// Disable.
  					disable = true;
  				}
  				else if (action == false) {
  					// Enable.
  					disable = false;
  				}
  				else {
  					// Called by an event.
  					if (document.forms[0].schedule_id) {
  						disable = document.forms[0].schedule_id.value;
  					}
  					else {
  						disable = false;
  					}
  				}
  				var output_format=document.getElementById('output_format_radio_buttons');
  				if (output_format) {
  					document.forms[0].output_format[0].checked=true;
  					output_format.style.display=(disable ? 'none': 'inline');
  				}
  			}

  			function PreResetProc() {
  				if (document.getElementById("vmd_vaa")) { document.getElementById("vmd_vaa").style.display = 'none'; }
  				if (document.getElementById("PreResetField").value === 'create_roa') {
  					document.getElementById('create_roa').checked = true;
  					document.getElementById('create_roa').disabled = false;
  					Disable_Tied_Checkbox('create_roa','create_appendix');
  					Disable_Tied_Checkbox('create_roa','create_abridged_docket_report');
  					Disable_Tied_Checkbox('create_roa','view_multi_docs');
  					show_roa(true);
  					show_appendix(false);
  					show_formats(true);
  					if (document.getElementById("court_user_roa")) {
  						Rest_Seal_Entries(false);
  					}
  				} else if(document.getElementById("PreResetField").value === 'create_appendix') {
  					document.getElementById('create_appendix').checked = true;
  					document.getElementById('create_appendix').disabled = false;
  					Disable_Tied_Checkbox('create_appendix','create_roa');
  					Disable_Tied_Checkbox('create_appendix','create_abridged_docket_report');
  					Disable_Tied_Checkbox('create_appendix','view_multi_docs');
  					if (document.getElementById('create_roa')) show_roa(false);
  					show_appendix(true);
  					show_formats(true);
  					if (document.getElementById("court_user")) {
  						Rest_Seal_Entries(false);
  					}
  				} else if(document.getElementById("PreResetField").value === 'view_multi_docs') {
  					document.getElementById('view_multi_docs').checked = true;
  					document.getElementById('view_multi_docs').disabled = false;
  					document.getElementById('pdf_header').disabled = false;
  					Disable_Tied_Checkbox('view_multi_docs','create_abridged_docket_report');
  					Disable_Tied_Checkbox('view_multi_docs','create_roa');
  					Disable_Tied_Checkbox('view_multi_docs','create_appendix');
  					show_formats(true);

  					if (document.getElementById("vmd_vaa")) { document.getElementById("vmd_vaa").style.display = 'inline'; }

  					Disable_Tied_Checkbox('create_abridged_docket_report', 'create_appendix');
  					show_formats(true);
  					if (document.getElementById('create_appendix')) show_appendix(false);

  							document.getElementById("restricted_entries").disabled = false;

  					if (document.getElementById('create_appendix')) {

  					if (document.getElementById('create_abridged_docket_report')) document.getElementById('create_abridged_docket_report').disabled = false;
  					show_formats(false);

  <SCRIPT LANGUAGE="JavaScript">
  		var timerId;
  		var BeenHere = 0;
  		IsForm  = true;
  		function empty(s) {
  			var whitespace = " \t\n\r";
  			if(s == null || s.length == 0) {
  				return(true);
  			}
  		    // Is s only whitespace characters?
  		    for (var i = 0; i < s.length; i++) {
  		        var c = s.charAt(i);
         			 if (whitespace.indexOf(c) == -1) return false;
  		    }
  			return(true);
  		}
  		function ClearTimer() {
  			BeenHere = 0;
  			clearTimeout(timerId);
  			return(true);
  		}
  		var FormId = 0;
  		function ProcessForm() {
  			if(BeenHere == 1) {
  				alert("Submission already made, please wait for response from server");
  				return(false);
  			}
  			BeenHere = 1;
  			timerId=setTimeout("ClearTimer()",5000);
  if( ! ValidateAllOnSubmit("CheckDate", 0) ) {ClearTimer();return false;}
  if( ! ValidateAllOnSubmit("CheckNumber", 0) ) {ClearTimer();return false;}
  document.forms[FormId].submit();return true
  }

  function RunAfterClear() {
  	
  }

  <script language="JavaScript">
  var AssignResetButtonTimeout;
  function AssignResetButton() {
  	if (AssignResetButtonTimeout)
  		window.clearTimeout(AssignResetButtonTimeout);

  	var resetButton = document.forms[0].reset;
  	if (resetButton && resetButton.value) {
  		var oldHandler = resetButton.onclick;
  		var newHandler = function() {setTimeout("RunAfterClear()", 100)};
  		resetButton.onclick = function() {
  			if (oldHandler) {
  				oldHandler();
  			}
  			newHandler();
  		}
  	}
  	else
  		AssignResetButtonTimeout = window.setTimeout(AssignResetButton, 1);
  }
  AssignResetButton();
  </script>

• I see why it’s still looping back to the form: that page has no named input for the case number, so posting case_number_text_area_0 is
  ignored. CM/ECF expects all_case_ids + a non‑blank case_num (and often a CASE_NUM cookie). Juriscraper’s approach for this is a direct POST
  to DktRpt.pl?1-L_1_0-1 with all_case_ids and case_num=" ".

  I’ve now added that as a direct fallback when the form flow still returns the request page, plus the CASE_NUM cookie. You’ll need to redeploy
  and re‑run the pull.

  What changed

  - Direct fallback POST to DktRpt.pl?1-L_1_0-1 using:
      - all_case_ids=<case_id>
      - case_num=" " (non‑blank)
      - date_from="1/1/1960" (to avoid the “big docket” confirm page)
      - multipart/form‑data
  - CASE_NUM cookie is now set to 3:25-cr-00076(41539) for this case format.

  		var IsForm = false;
  		var FirstField;
  		function SetFocus() {
  			if(IsForm) {
  				if(FirstField) {
  					var ind = FirstField.indexOf('document.',0);
  					if(ind == 0)
  					{
  						eval(FirstField);
  					}
  					else
  					{
  						var Code = "document.forms[0]."+FirstField+".focus();";
  						eval(Code);
  					}
  				} else {
  					var Cnt = 0;
  					while(document.forms[0].elements[Cnt] != null) {
  						try {
  							if(document.forms[0].elements[Cnt].type != "hidden" &&
  									!document.forms[0].elements[Cnt].disabled &&
  									!document.forms[0].elements[Cnt].readOnly) {
  								document.forms[0].elements[Cnt].focus();
  								break;
  							}
  						}
  						catch(e) {}
  						Cnt += 1;
  					}
  				}
  			}
  			return(true);
  		}

      <SCRIPT>
      function ValidateAllOnSubmit(function_name,form_num) {
          if(form_num == null) form_num = 0; // default if not provided
          var f = document.forms[form_num];  // f is the form object

  	// anticipate programmer errors - if no quotes around 1st param, its a function reference
  	if(typeof(function_name) == "function")
  	    function_name = function_name.toString().match(/function\s+([^\(]+)/)[1];

  	// iterate through all the elements of the form
  	for(var i=0; i<f.length; i++)   {
  	    var e=f.elements[i];
  	    if (e.type=="text"  || e.type=="textarea") {
  		// adding foo on to onchange property of form element[i]
  		// because cant be null for pattern match
  		var msg=(e.onchange)+"foo";

  		// if the onchange attribute matches the function name (and optionally an arg list)
  		re = new RegExp(function_name+"(\\s*\\([^)]+\\))?"); // think of each \\ as \
  		var match = msg.match(re);
  		if  (match) {
                      function_call = match[0];

  		    // Execute validation function in question and see if it failed
                      function_call = function_call.replace(/this/g
                                             , "document.forms["+form_num+"].elements["+i+"]");
                      if(! eval(function_call)) {
  			e.focus();
  			return(false);
  		    }
  		}
  	    }
  	}
  	return(1);
      }
      </SCRIPT>

  			var show_formats = function (action) {
  				var disable = false;
  				if (action == true) {
  					// Disable.
  					disable = true;
  				}
  				else if (action == false) {
  					// Enable.
  					disable = false;
  				}
  				else {
  					// Called by an event.
  					if (document.forms[0].schedule_id) {
  						disable = document.forms[0].schedule_id.value;
  					}
  					else {
  						disable = false;
  					}
  				}

  				if (output_format) {
  					document.forms[0].output_format[0].checked=true;
  					output_format.style.display=(disable ? 'none': 'inline');
  				}
  			}

  			function PreResetProc() {
  				if (document.getElementById("vmd_vaa")) { document.getElementById("vmd_vaa").style.display = 'none'; }
  				if (document.getElementById("PreResetField").value === 'create_roa') {

  					show_formats(true);

  					Disable_Tied_Checkbox('create_appendix','create_abridged_docket_report');

  					show_appendix(true);

  						Rest_Seal_Entries(false);
  					}
  				} else if(document.getElementById("PreResetField").value === 'view_multi_docs') {
  					document.getElementById('view_multi_docs').checked = true;
  					document.getElementById('view_multi_docs').disabled = false;
  					document.getElementById('pdf_header').disabled = false;

  <SCRIPT LANGUAGE="JavaScript">
  		var timerId;
  		var BeenHere = 0;
  		IsForm  = true;
  		function empty(s) {
  			var whitespace = " \t\n\r";
  			if(s == null || s.length == 0) {
  				return(true);
  			}
  		    // Is s only whitespace characters?
  		    for (var i = 0; i < s.length; i++) {
  		        var c = s.charAt(i);
         			 if (whitespace.indexOf(c) == -1) return false;
  		    }
  			return(true);
  		}
  		function ClearTimer() {
  			BeenHere = 0;
  			clearTimeout(timerId);
  			return(true);
  		}
  		var FormId = 0;
  		function ProcessForm() {
  			if(BeenHere == 1) {
  				alert("Submission already made, please wait for response from server");
  				return(false);
  			}
  			BeenHere = 1;
  			timerId=setTimeout("ClearTimer()",5000);
  if( ! ValidateAllOnSubmit("CheckDate", 0) ) {ClearTimer();return false;}
  if( ! ValidateAllOnSubmit("CheckNumber", 0) ) {ClearTimer();return false;}
  document.forms[FormId].submit();return true
  }

  function RunAfterClear() {
  	
  }

  <script language="JavaScript">
  var AssignResetButtonTimeout;
  function AssignResetButton() {
  	if (AssignResetButtonTimeout)
  		window.clearTimeout(AssignResetButtonTimeout);

  	var resetButton = document.forms[0].reset;
  	if (resetButton && resetButton.value) {
  		var oldHandler = resetButton.onclick;
  		var newHandler = function() {setTimeout("RunAfterClear()", 100)};
  		resetButton.onclick = function() {
  			if (oldHandler) {
  				oldHandler();
  			}
  			newHandler();
  		}

     971
     972 +def _extract_judge_fields_from_text(text: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
     973 +    if not text:
     974 +        return {}
     975 +    lines = [line.strip() for line in text.splitlines() if line.strip()]
     976 +    assigned: List[str] = []
     977 +    referred: List[str] = []
     978 +    presiding: List[str] = []
     979 +    for line in lines:
     980 +        match = re.search(r"Assigned to:\s*(.+)", line, re.IGNORECASE)
     981 +        if match:
     982 +            assigned.append(match.group(1).strip())
     983 +            continue
     984 +        match = re.search(r"Referred to:\s*(.+)", line, re.IGNORECASE)
     985 +        if match:
     986 +            referred.append(match.group(1).strip())
     987 +            continue
     988 +        match = re.search(r"Presiding Judge:\s*(.+)", line, re.IGNORECASE)
     989 +        if match:
     990 +            presiding.append(match.group(1).strip())
     991 +            continue
     992 +    judges = []
     993 +    for value in assigned + referred + presiding:
     994 +        if value and value not in judges:
     995 +            judges.append(value)
     996 +    output: Dict[str, Any] = {}
     997 +    if assigned:
     998 +        output["assigned_to"] = assigned
     999 +    if referred:
    1000 +        output["referred_to"] = referred
    1001 +    if presiding:
    1002 +        output["presiding_judge"] = presiding
    1003 +    if judges:
    1004 +        output["judges"] = judges
    1005 +    return output
